<p><span style=&quot;vertical-align: inherit;&quot;>Good morning, skiers and riders, welcome to the Eldora Snow Report for Sunday, December 12, 2021.</span></p>
<p>Our snowmakers and groomers have been burning the midnight oil to get new terrain open, and today we're excited to announce that the Indian Peaks chairlift will open, serving City Lights, Around The Horn Trail, and Lower Ambush trails. Over on the lower mountain, we've added to our beginner terrain offerings with the opening of the Tenderfoot carpet lift, as well as Foxtail, Uncle Bob's, and Little Hawk trails.</p>
<p>Don't forget that we're offering FREE rides to and from Boulder today. Scroll down to see the schedule.</p>
<p>Today, we can expect sunny skies, with the high near 46 and temps falling in the afternoon and a west southwest wind 13 to 21 miles per hour, with gusts as high as 33 miles per hour.&amp;nbsp; &amp;nbsp; &amp;nbsp;</p>
<p>W<span style=&quot;vertical-align: inherit;&quot;>e're still experiencing early-season conditions out there, so always remember that smart and safe skiing and riding is the goal today and every day this winter. No matter your age or ability, ski and ride slowly and respectfully, staying aware of your surroundings and always following <a href=&quot;https://www.coloradoski.com/safety/know-your-code&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; rel=&quot;noopener&quot;><strong>Your Responsibility Code</strong></a>. Here are the seven points to the Code:</span></p>
<ul>
<li><span style=&quot;vertical-align: inherit;&quot;>Always stay in control, and be able to stop or avoid other people or objects.</span></li>
<li><span style=&quot;vertical-align: inherit;&quot;>People ahead of you have the right of way. It is your responsibility to avoid them.</span></li>
<li><span style=&quot;vertical-align: inherit;&quot;>You must not stop where you obstruct a trail, or are not visible from above.</span></li>
<li><span style=&quot;vertical-align: inherit;&quot;>Whenever starting downhill or merging into a trail, look uphill and yield to others.</span></li>
<li><span style=&quot;vertical-align: inherit;&quot;>Always use devices to help prevent runaway equipment.</span></li>
<li><span style=&quot;vertical-align: inherit;&quot;>Observe all posted signs and warnings. Keep off closed trails and out of closed areas.</span></li>
<li><span style=&quot;vertical-align: inherit;&quot;>Prior to using any lift, you must have the knowledge and ability to load, ride and unload safely.</span></li>
</ul>
<p><span style=&quot;vertical-align: inherit;&quot;>Here's what's available today:</span></p>
<ul>
<li><span style=&quot;text-decoration: underline;&quot;><strong>Open Lifts</strong></span><br />Alpenglow<br />Race<br />EZ<br />Tenderfoot<br />Indian Peaks<br /><br /></li>
<li><span style=&quot;text-decoration: underline;&quot;><strong>Open Trails</strong></span><br />Hornblower<br />Windmill<br />International<br />La Belle<br />Hot Dog Alley<br />Chute<br />Bunnyfair<br />Ryder's<br />Sundance<br />Foxtail<br />Uncle Bob's<br />Little Hawk<br />Lower Ambush<br />Citylights<br />Around The Horn<br /><br /></li>
<li style=&quot;text-align: left;&quot;><span style=&quot;text-decoration: underline;&quot;><strong>Woodward Terrain Parks</strong></span><br />Timbers Park<br />Ryder's<br />Sundance</li>
</ul>
<p><strong><a href=&quot;https://www.eldora.com/the-mountain/trail-area-maps/alpine-trail-map&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; rel=&quot;noopener&quot;>Click here to see a trail map</a></strong>.</p>
<p>FREE RIDES TODAY! Remember, we're offering free rides to Eldora from Boulder today. Please help us reduce traffic and emissions and conserve parking spaces by utilizing this convenient service.</p>
<p>Westbound departures from Boulder County Justice Center parking lot (1777 6th St, Boulder, CO 80302) to Eldora:</p>
<ul>

<li>9:00 AM</li>
<li>11:00 AM</li>

<ul>

<p><strong><span style=&quot;vertical-align: inherit;&quot;>Early-Season Conditions:</span></strong><span style=&quot;vertical-align: inherit;&quot;> Always remember that smart and safe skiing and riding is the goal every day this winter. No matter your age or ability, ski and ride slowly and respectfully, staying aware of your surroundings and always following </span><a href=&quot;https://www.coloradoski.com/safety/know-your-code&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; rel=&quot;noopener&quot;><span style=&quot;vertical-align: inherit;&quot;><strong>Your Responsibility Code</strong></span></a><span style=&quot;vertical-align: inherit;&quot;>.</span></p>
<p><strong><span style=&quot;vertical-align: inherit;&quot;>Parking at Eldora:</span></strong><span style=&quot;vertical-align: inherit;&quot;> Parking can be a hot commodity on weekends and holidays at Eldora, so be sure to read up on the tips and tricks on our <a href=&quot;https://www.eldora.com/plan-your-trip/getting-here/closer-to-you&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; rel=&quot;noopener&quot;><strong>GETTING HERE</strong></a>&amp;nbsp;page. The best way to ensure a smooth arrival experience is to avoid &quot;peak-visitation&quot; periods like weekend and holiday mornings and aim to visit on afternoons and weekdays.</span></p>
<p><strong><span style=&quot;vertical-align: inherit;&quot;>Sustainable Transportation:</span></strong><span style=&quot;vertical-align: inherit;&quot;> You can also help keep Eldora accessible for all by carpooling instead of driving by yourself, riding </span><strong><a href=&quot;https://www.rtd-denver.com/app/route/NB/schedule?day=saturday&amp;amp;direction=westbound&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; rel=&quot;noopener&quot;><span style=&quot;vertical-align: inherit;&quot;>RTD's NB bus</span></a></strong><span style=&quot;vertical-align: inherit;&quot;>, or taking one of our FREE weekend/holiday shuttles from the&amp;nbsp;</span><strong><a href=&quot;https://www.google.com/maps/place/Boulder+County+Justice+Center/@40.0300748,-105.2981147,14z/data=!4m5!3m4!1s0x876bec221c9e38fb:0xed0fa17137f67dbc!8m2!3d40.0146575!4d-105.2874437&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; rel=&quot;noopener&quot;><span style=&quot;vertical-align: inherit;&quot;>Boulder County Justice Center parking lot</span></a></strong><span style=&quot;vertical-align: inherit;&quot;> to Eldora. View the shuttle schedule on our </span><strong><a href=&quot;https://www.eldora.com/plan-your-trip/getting-here/closer-to-you&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; rel=&quot;noopener&quot;><span style=&quot;vertical-align: inherit;&quot;>Getting Here</span></a></strong><span style=&quot;vertical-align: inherit;&quot;> page.</span></p>
<p><strong><span style=&quot;vertical-align: inherit;&quot;>Single-Occupancy Vehicle (SOV) Fee:</span></strong><span style=&quot;vertical-align: inherit;&quot;> New this winter, Boulder County is requiring Eldora to charge SOVs $ 10 to park on weekends and holiday periods. These fees will begin on December 18, and will not be charged on non-holiday weekdays. Fees collected will directly fund our Sustainable Transportation Program, which includes free round-trip shuttles from Boulder and free round-trip RTD tickets for Eldora-bound riders from Boulder. Learn more </span><strong><a href=&quot;https://www.eldora.com/plan-your-trip/getting-here/closer-to-you&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; rel=&quot;noopener&quot;><span style=&quot;vertical-align: inherit;&quot;>HERE</span></a></strong><span style=&quot;vertical-align: inherit;&quot;>.</span></p>
<p><strong><span style=&quot;vertical-align: inherit;&quot;>Non-Alpine Operations:</span></strong><span style=&quot;vertical-align: inherit;&quot;> Our cross-country skiing, uphill skiing, and snowshoeing operations are not online yet, but we hope to have them up and running as soon as conditions allow.</span></p>
<p><span style=&quot;vertical-align: inherit;&quot;><strong>We're Hiring! </strong>We've increased wages for many positions and we're actively hiring in all departments. Browse jobs and apply today at <a href=&quot;https://www.eldora.com/culture/employment/employment-at-eldora&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; rel=&quot;noopener&quot;><strong>Eldora.com/jobs</strong></a>. Staffing shortages may affect our service offerings this winter, and we appreciate your understanding. <br /> <br /><strong>Stay Informed:</strong> Before leaving home this winter, always check <a href=&quot;https://www.eldora.com/the-mountain/conditions-weather/current-conditions-forecast&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; rel=&quot;noopener&quot;><strong>Eldora.com/conditions</strong></a> for important weather and operational announcements. Sign up for text alerts by texting ELDORA to 855-623-6005 to stay in the know. Follow us on <a href=&quot;https://www.facebook.com/eldoramountainresort/&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; rel=&quot;noopener&quot;><strong>Facebook</strong></a>, <a href=&quot;https://twitter.com/eldoramtnresort&quot;><strong>Twitter</strong></a>, and <a href=&quot;https://www.instagram.com/eldoramtnresort/&quot;><strong>Instagram</strong></a>.</span></p>
<p><span style=&quot;vertical-align: inherit;&quot;>For detailed information on early-season visits to Eldora, please visit the latest </span><strong><a href=&quot;https://www.eldora.com/culture/blog-and-news/blogs-and-news/eldora-opens-111921&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; rel=&quot;noopener&quot;><span style=&quot;vertical-align: inherit;&quot;>blog post</span></a></strong><span style=&quot;vertical-align: inherit;&quot;> on our website and always stay tuned to this page for important weather information and operational updates.</span></p>

<p><strong><a href="https://www.eldora.com/the-mountain/trail-area-maps/alpine-trail-map" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Click here to see a trail map</a></strong>.</p>
<p>FREE RIDES TODAY! Remember, we're offering free rides to Eldora from Boulder today. Please help us reduce traffic and emissions and conserve parking spaces by utilizing this convenient service.</p>
<p>Westbound departures from Boulder County Justice Center parking lot (1777 6th St, Boulder, CO 80302) to Eldora:</p>
<ul>
<li>7:00 AM</li>
<li>9:00 AM</li>
<li>11:00 AM</li>
</ul>
<p>Eastbound departures from Eldora, back to Justice Center:</p>
<ul>
<li>1:00 PM</li>
<li>3:00 PM</li>
<li>4:00 PM</li>
</ul>
<p><span style="vertical-align: inherit;">For the complete snow and conditions report, please visit us online at </span><strong><a href="http://www.eldora.com/conditions" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="vertical-align: inherit;">Eldora.com/conditions.</span></a></strong></p>
<p><span style="vertical-align: inherit;">Thanks for checking the Eldora snow report. We'll see you on the hill!</span></p>
<p><span style="vertical-align: inherit;">---&nbsp;</span></p>
<p><strong><span style="vertical-align: inherit;">Early-Season Conditions:</span></strong><span style="vertical-align: inherit;"> Always remember that smart and safe skiing and riding is the goal every day this winter. No matter your age or ability, ski and ride slowly and respectfully, staying aware of your surroundings and always following </span><a href="https://www.coloradoski.com/safety/know-your-code" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="vertical-align: inherit;"><strong>Your Responsibility Code</strong></span></a><span style="vertical-align: inherit;">.</span></p>
<p><strong><span style="vertical-align: inherit;">Parking at Eldora:</span></strong><span style="vertical-align: inherit;"> Parking can be a hot commodity on weekends and holidays at Eldora, so be sure to read up on the tips and tricks on our <a href="https://www.eldora.com/plan-your-trip/getting-here/closer-to-you" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><strong>GETTING HERE</strong></a>&nbsp;page. The best way to ensure a smooth arrival experience is to avoid "peak-visitation" periods like weekend and holiday mornings and aim to visit on afternoons and weekdays.</span></p>
<p><strong><span style="vertical-align: inherit;">Sustainable Transportation:</span></strong><span style="vertical-align: inherit;"> You can also help keep Eldora accessible for all by carpooling instead of driving by yourself, riding </span><strong><a href="https://www.rtd-denver.com/app/route/NB/schedule?day=saturday&amp;direction=westbound" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="vertical-align: inherit;">RTD's NB bus</span></a></strong><span style="vertical-align: inherit;">, or taking one of our FREE weekend/holiday shuttles from the&nbsp;</span><strong><a href="https://www.google.com/maps/place/Boulder+County+Justice+Center/@40.0300748,-105.2981147,14z/data=!4m5!3m4!1s0x876bec221c9e38fb:0xed0fa17137f67dbc!8m2!3d40.0146575!4d-105.2874437" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="vertical-align: inherit;">Boulder County Justice Center parking lot</span></a></strong><span style="vertical-align: inherit;"> to Eldora. View the shuttle schedule on our </span><strong><a href="https://www.eldora.com/plan-your-trip/getting-here/closer-to-you" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="vertical-align: inherit;">Getting Here</span></a></strong><span style="vertical-align: inherit;"> page.</span></p>
<p><strong><span style="vertical-align: inherit;">Single-Occupancy Vehicle (SOV) Fee:</span></strong><span style="vertical-align: inherit;"> New this winter, Boulder County is requiring Eldora to charge SOVs $ 10 to park on weekends and holiday periods. These fees will begin on December 18, and will not be charged on non-holiday weekdays. Fees collected will directly fund our Sustainable Transportation Program, which includes free round-trip shuttles from Boulder and free round-trip RTD tickets for Eldora-bound riders from Boulder. Learn more </span><strong><a href="https://www.eldora.com/plan-your-trip/getting-here/closer-to-you" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="vertical-align: inherit;">HERE</span></a></strong><span style="vertical-align: inherit;">.</span></p>
<p><strong><span style="vertical-align: inherit;">Non-Alpine Operations:</span></strong><span style="vertical-align: inherit;"> Our cross-country skiing, uphill skiing, and snowshoeing operations are not online yet, but we hope to have them up and running as soon as conditions allow.</span></p>
<p><span style="vertical-align: inherit;"><strong>We're Hiring! </strong>We've increased wages for many positions and we're actively hiring in all departments. Browse jobs and apply today at <a href="https://www.eldora.com/culture/employment/employment-at-eldora" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><strong>Eldora.com/jobs</strong></a>. Staffing shortages may affect our service offerings this winter, and we appreciate your understanding. <br> <br><strong>Stay Informed:</strong> Before leaving home this winter, always check <a href="https://www.eldora.com/the-mountain/conditions-weather/current-conditions-forecast" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><strong>Eldora.com/conditions</strong></a> for important weather and operational announcements. Sign up for text alerts by texting ELDORA to 855-623-6005 to stay in the know. Follow us on <a href="https://www.facebook.com/eldoramountainresort/" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><strong>Facebook</strong></a>, <a href="https://twitter.com/eldoramtnresort"><strong>Twitter</strong></a>, and <a href="https://www.instagram.com/eldoramtnresort/"><strong>Instagram</strong></a>.</span></p>
<p><span style="vertical-align: inherit;">For detailed information on early-season visits to Eldora, please visit the latest </span><strong><a href="https://www.eldora.com/culture/blog-and-news/blogs-and-news/eldora-opens-111921" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="vertical-align: inherit;">blog post</span></a></strong><span style="vertical-align: inherit;"> on our website and always stay tuned to this page for important weather information and operational updates.</span></p>
